    SELECT TOP(1) [u].[Id], [u].[Email], [u].[MobileNumber], [u].[Name], [u].[Role]
    FROM [Users] AS [u]
    WHERE [u].[Id] = @__userId_0
) AS [u0]
LEFT JOIN [Cars] AS [c] ON [u0].[Id] = [c].[CustId]
ORDER BY [u0].[Id]
